theorem nilpotent_plus_one_is_unit {R : Type*} [ring R] {x : R} (hx : is_nilpotent x) : is_unit (1 + x) :=
begin
  obtain ‚ü®n, hn‚ü© := hx,
  use (1 - x + x^2 - x^3 + ... + (-1)^(n-1) * x^(n-1)),
  split,
  { calc
      (1 + x) * (1 - x + x^2 - x^3 + ... + (-1)^(n-1) * x^(n-1))
          = 1 - x^n : by ring
      ... = 1 : by rw hn },
  { calc
      (1 - x + x^2 - x^3 + ... + (-1)^(n-1) * x^(n-1)) * (1 + x)
          = 1 - x^n : by ring
      ... = 1 : by rw hn }
end

done

theorem union_of_subspaces_is_subspace_iff_one_is_contained_in_other 
  {F : Type*} [field F] {V : Type*} [add_comm_group V] [module F V] 
  (U‚ÇÅ U‚ÇÇ : submodule F V) : 
  submodule F V :=
begin
  split,
  { intro h,
    by_cases h‚ÇÅ : U‚ÇÅ ‚â§ U‚ÇÇ,
    { left, exact h‚ÇÅ },
    { right, 
      have h‚ÇÇ : U‚ÇÇ ‚â§ U‚ÇÅ,
      { intros x hx,
        by_contradiction hcontra,
        have : x ‚àà (U‚ÇÅ ‚äî U‚ÇÇ) := submodule.mem_sup_right hx,
        rw h at this,
        exact hcontra this },
      exact h‚ÇÇ } },
  { rintro (h‚ÇÅ | h‚ÇÇ),
    { rw submodule.sup_eq_right.mpr h‚ÇÅ },
    { rw submodule.sup_eq_left.mpr h‚ÇÇ } }
end

done
